  <script>
     const acceptedLocales = [
      'en-au',
      'en-ca',
      'en-gb',
      'en-in',
      'en-us',
      'de-de',
      'es-es',
      'es-la',
      'fr-fr',
      'it-it',
      'ja-jp',
      'ko-kr',
      'pt-br',
      'zh-tw',
      'zh-cn',
    ];
    const orphanLocales = [
      'ru-ru',
      'sv-se',
      'nl-nl',
      'vi-vn',
      'th-th',
      'id-id',
    ];
    const ignoreList = [
      'apps',
      'docs',
      'rate-limit-test',
      'rss',
    ]
    function getPathFromLocale(locale, code, pathString) {
      if ( locale === code || !acceptedLocales.includes(code) || acceptedLocales.includes(locale) || orphanLocales.includes(locale) ) {
        return null;
      } else {
        return [code, locale ? locale : '', pathString].filter(part => part !== '').join('/');
      }
    };
    if (localStorage.getItem('langPreference')) {
      if (localStorage.getItem('langPreference').toLowerCase() != 'en-us') {
          const langPreference = localStorage.getItem('langPreference').toLowerCase();
          const splitPath = window.location.pathname.split('/').filter(part => part !== '');
          const currentLang = splitPath[0];
          if (!acceptedLocales.includes(currentLang) && !orphanLocales.includes(currentLang) && !ignoreList.includes(splitPath[0])) {
            splitPath.splice(0, 0, langPreference.toLowerCase());
            const newUrl = 'https://' + window.location.hostname + '/' + splitPath.join('/') + '/' + window.location.search;
            window.location.replace(newUrl);   
          }
        }
    } else if (!window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().includes('googlebot')) {
        const requestedLang = window.navigator.language;
        const splitPath = window.location.pathname.split('/').filter(part => part !== '');
        const maybeLocale = splitPath.shift();
        const splitPathString = splitPath.join('/');

        if (requestedLang && requestedLang.toLowerCase() != "en-us") {
          const requestedLangCode = requestedLang
            .toLowerCase()
            .replace('_', '-');
          const redirectPath = getPathFromLocale(maybeLocale, requestedLangCode, splitPathString);
          if (redirectPath && !ignoreList.includes(maybeLocale)) {
            window.location.replace('https://' + window.location.hostname + '/' + redirectPath + '/' + window.location.search);
          }
        }
      }
    </script>

       <h1 class="marketing-product-h1">Secure your remote workforce</h1> 
       <p class="text--bolder">Cloudflare for Teams provides security without slowdown</p> 
       <p>Your workforce has expanded to include remote employees, contractors, and vendors. All require secure access to internal applications and tools — no matter where in the world they’re working from.</p> 
       <p>Cloudflare for Teams enables seamless, Zero Trust application access and software-defined security, allowing you to secure your remote teams, devices, and data without sacrificing performance or user experience.</p>

   <section id="what-s-slowing-down-your-workforce-" class="tile three-features-blade tile--no-bottom-padding-desktop tile__background--white text--black"> 
    <section class="tile__content tile__content--1200px"> 
     <div class="grid"> 
      <h2 class="page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__header">What's slowing down your workforce?</h2> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--third page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail flex flex-column page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail--left"> 
       <div> 
        <img class="image--three-feature-icon" title="icon network scale blue 48px" alt="icon network scale blue 48px" src="/resources/images/slt3lc6tev37/7CzpRaPu9MRLDfD4xFpmWE/61383ce49be50c63955f6327ee1ddf1a/icon_network-scale_blue_48px.svg"> 
       </div> 
       <h3 class="page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail__header">Legacy security tools don’t scale</h3> 
       <div class="page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail__copy"> 
        <p>The larger and more distributed your workforce becomes, the harder it is to secure remote users, devices, and data. Legacy security tools, like hardware firewalls and VPNs, are not built to handle hybrid infrastructure, remote teams, or a constantly-evolving threat landscape.</p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--third page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail flex flex-column page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail--left"> 
       <div> 
        <img class="image--three-feature-icon" title="icon connect 3 blue 48px" alt="icon connect 3 blue 48px" src="/resources/images/slt3lc6tev37/33GNJqvGvxFGKoIUAnvthw/58e8866ef112382d56676902de021782/icon_connect-3_blue_48px.svg"> 
       </div> 
       <h3 class="page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail__header">VPNs impact performance</h3> 
       <div class="page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail__copy"> 
        <p>By design, VPNs trombone all traffic to and from central on-premise appliances. Even when everything runs smoothly, global teams still experience latency when accessing internal tools and data — not only affecting productivity, but user experience as well.</p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--third page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail flex flex-column page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail--left"> 
       <div> 
        <img class="image--three-feature-icon" title="teams security shield zero trust blue 80px" alt="teams security shield zero trust blue 80px" src="/resources/images/slt3lc6tev37/6XGYSR66UbDyADSnXT2H2x/f4774d4563c250a87a1c1472d9885aca/teams-security-shield-zero-trust_blue_80px.svg"> 
       </div> 
       <h3 class="page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail__header">User are vulnerable to security threats</h3> 
       <div class="page-cms__icon-with-text-bot__detail__copy"> 
        <p>Remote employees use a wide range of devices — from work-issued computers to personal phones and tablets — to access company resources. Without proactive threat protection in place, IT departments lack the visibility and ability to safeguard these employee devices from cyberattacks.</p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </section> 
   </section> 
   <section class="tile image-text-horizontal-blade  tile__background--light-blue text--black tile--no-bottom-padding"> 
    <section class="tile__content tile__content--1200px"> 
     <div class="grid grid--vertical-center"> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half-desktop page-cms__image-with-text__image-grid page-cms__image-with-text__image-grid--left"> 
       <img class="responsive-image" title="teams access improvement plan 1" alt="teams access improvement plan 1" src="/resources/images/slt3lc6tev37/1310xjEU9gSfZkQZbZ5gtM/cde3694470c662ac835de0bfb7bb03cc/teams-access-improvement-plan_1.svg"> 
      </div> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half-desktop"> 
       <h2 class="page-cms__image-with-text__header">Expand your security perimeter to fit your workforce</h2> 
       <p>Hardware limitations shouldn’t dictate the strength of your security posture. As your remote workforce expands beyond on-premise offices and devices, you need security tools that can scale alongside it.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </section> 
   </section> 
   <section class="tile image-text-horizontal-blade  tile__background--light-blue text--black tile--no-bottom-padding"> 
    <section class="tile__content tile__content--1200px"> 
     <div class="grid grid--vertical-center"> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half-desktop page-cms__image-with-text__image-grid page-cms__image-with-text__image-grid--right"> 
       <img class="responsive-image" title="network map spot hero" alt="network map spot hero" src="/resources/images/slt3lc6tev37/3IDrs7SGgWWNpWgxe2KKgt/b199f3efa6cf36bd9bef25c15f2b210d/network-map-spot-hero.svg"> 
      </div> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half-desktop"> 
       <h2 class="page-cms__image-with-text__header">Swap slow VPNs for a global edge network</h2> 
       <p>Modern enterprises require solutions capable of securing user access to on-premise, cloud-based, and SaaS applications from any location. Eliminate the headache of maintaining slow, outdated VPN infrastructure by authenticating and securing employee tools using a global edge network — accessible from wherever your users are located.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </section> 
   </section> 
   <section class="tile image-text-horizontal-blade  tile__background--light-blue text--black tile--no-bottom-padding"> 
    <section class="tile__content tile__content--1200px"> 
     <div class="grid grid--vertical-center"> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half-desktop page-cms__image-with-text__image-grid page-cms__image-with-text__image-grid--left"> 
       <img class="responsive-image" title="teams access zero trust 1" alt="teams access zero trust 1" src="/resources/images/slt3lc6tev37/64rkzfRlSKZAYVL0p5jiem/f5e23a2ea18da3ab323c68dbafc4253a/teams-access-zero-trust_1.svg"> 
      </div> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half-desktop"> 
       <h2 class="page-cms__image-with-text__header">Protect all applications with Zero Trust access policies</h2> 
       <p>The Zero Trust model requires user identity and multiple contextual factors to authorize access, making it difficult for attackers to impersonate employees and gain access to internal resources.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </section> 
   </section>

       <h2 class="page-cms__image-with-text__header">Protect against data loss and phishing</h2>

       <h2 class="marketing-product-h1">How Cloudflare secures remote teams</h2> 
       <div class="button-container button-container--no-bottom-margin"> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half"> 
       <p>Backed by a global network that spans 200+ cities worldwide, Cloudflare for Teams helps safeguard remote teams, devices, and corporate applications without degrading performance or introducing complex management systems.</p> 
       <div class="button-container button-container--no-bottom-margin">

   <section class="tile image-text-horizontal-blade  tile__background--white text--black tile--no-top-bottom-padding"> 
    <section class="tile__content tile__content--1200px"> 
     <div class="grid grid--vertical-center"> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half-desktop page-cms__image-with-text__image-grid page-cms__image-with-text__image-grid--right"> 
       <img class="responsive-image" title="teams access one dash" alt="teams access one dash" src="/resources/images/slt3lc6tev37/22qJBeY3tx1zlrnpAPJiSp/f79f52205c9b5f52064307b0900baf53/teams-access-one-dash.svg"> 
      </div> 
      <div class="grid__item grid__item--half-desktop"> 
       <p><img src="/resources/images/slt3lc6tev37/7LYQWx4BmUYrsEi7cnXMWN/d67c0b317d56674f43421f39221ca605/logo_cloudflare-access_color.svg" alt="logo cloudflare-access color svg"></p> 
       <p>Cloudflare Access places our global edge network in front of your internal applications, eliminating the latency issues remote users often experience with VPN clients. With Zero Trust access controls, every request to your applications is evaluated for user identity and device context before it is authorized.</p> 
       <div class="argo-tunnel__button-container button-container button-container--no-bottom-margin"> <a data-lis-enabled="true" data-lis-url="" data-lis-text="" href="/teams-access/" class="button button--blue button--inline button--margin-right button--stack-mobile cloudflare-magic-transit-modal">Learn more</a> 
       </div>

     </div> 
    </section>
   </section>
